### Step 5: Estimate the Property Value

- The 7-carbon chain in CCCCCCC(=O)OCC suggests a lipophilic contribution similar to CCCCCCCI (0.0680988), but the ester group will make it less lipophilic (higher property value) than a pure hydrocarbon or halogenated alkane.

- Ethyl acetate (2 carbons) = 0.34277832
- Ethyl heptanoate (7 carbons) = ?
- Methyl nonanoate (9 carbons) = -0.55548869
